<clause id="scl-cat-programmes-schemes" obligation="normative">
<title>Categories of Programmes and Schemes</title>
<p id="_6ab2773b-dc4d-818c-5104-e1d671e6c444">Categories of programmes and schemes for hydrographic and cartographic personnel are defined with respect to the theoretical background and working knowledge of those who successfully graduate from such programmes. The following programmes and schemes are eligible for international recognition by the FIG/IHO/ICA IBSC:</p>

<clause id="_category_a_programmes" obligation="normative">
000222_level_of_​knowledgeHanging paragraph in clause
<clause id="_level_of_knowledge" obligation="normative">
<title>Level of Knowledge</title>
<p id="_b9f604a6-1530-9e49-0cb7-ff5402f19b7c">Bloom’s taxonomy has been used as the basis to describe each intended learning outcome of the Standards and the associated verbs are an indication of the expected level of knowledge. One of the three following levels of knowledge is associated with each element of the S-5A/B and S-8A/B.</p>

<clause id="_3" obligation="normative">
000250_minimum_​duration_​of_​programmesHanging paragraph in clause
<clause id="_minimum_duration_of_programmes" obligation="normative">
<title>Minimum Duration of Programmes</title>
<p id="_58d5656a-8a76-a87c-7377-4330fa5f6e64">The minimum duration of Programmes must be sufficient to allow students to absorb the knowledge through the lectures, tutorials, self-study, practical exercises and the final project. In the experience of the Board, to achieve the above, for a programme (without exemptions sought) delivered full-time in a continuous manner an expected minimum time frame is:</p>

<clause id="_6" obligation="normative">
000264_​practical_​exercises_and_​final_projectHanging paragraph in clause
<clause id="_practical_exercises_and_final_project" obligation="normative">
<title>PRACTICAL EXERCISES AND FINAL PROJECT</title>
<p id="_6f97ae17-2542-310a-668f-5e61f7750a2b">Because hydrography and nautical cartography are applied disciplines, every student undertaking a Category “A” or Category “B” Programme is expected to receive hands-on experience under direct supervision of the instructors. This experience should form an important part of the student’s assessment, and should be considered in two parts, practical exercises and a final project.</p>

<clause id="scl-practical-exercises" obligation="normative">
000306cl-professional-cert­ificationHanging paragraph in clause
<clause id="cl-professional-certification" obligation="normative">
<title>PROFESSIONAL CERTIFICATION OR INDIVIDUAL RECOGNITION SCHEMES</title>
<p id="_869f1fc5-c0bf-c3b9-f3f5-0a7fd120abf0">The Board <em>does not provide recognition to individuals</em> directly. It does however seek to recognize formal systems and schemes that review and assess individuals’ experience in order to provide them with professional certification or individual recognition of their Competency. These Schemes offer to monitor and assess individuals at regular intervals and to register them in a formal system so that an individual may gain professional certification or individual recognition at a defined level of competency which may include Category “A” and Category “B”.</p>

<clause id="_background_board_philosophy_and_process_concerning_schemes_for_professional_certification_of_individual_recognition" obligation="normative">
000440_​documentation_to_​be_​submittedHanging paragraph in clause
<clause id="_documentation_to_be_submitted" obligation="normative">
<title>Documentation to be submitted</title>
<p id="_c0c24d68-a9f5-ae67-b1fd-06ac371e2d4b">See <xref target="annex-submitting-institutions"/>: <strong>S-5A/B and S-8A/B</strong> Checklist for Submitting Institutions. The checklist will assist the submitting institution in ensuring all documentation is included.</p>

<p id="_d6aa885e-e56d-34ef-32a3-c767ffc2f910">It is the experience of the Board that a well-prepared submission is one of clarity with detailed cross-referencing of the submitted programme syllabus to the content and learning outcomes provided in the standards.</p>
